Large Woodworking Plant Established on Kamchatka Island 96

TASS News Agency, Kamchatka, 10th – The Soviet Union is establishing a large-scale combined woodworking plant on this island. It will commence operations this summer. The total value of the plant is approximately 5 million rubles and includes a sawmill, a barrel-making department capable of producing 300,000 barrels annually, and a box-making department capable of producing 2 million wooden boxes annually. The plant will require 600 workers and will include a hospital, a public bathhouse, a laundry, a public canteen, and a bakery. The main purpose of the plant is to manufacture barrels to meet the needs of the Soviet Far East coast fishing industry. Its production value this year is expected to reach 7 million rubles.

Important News

League of Nations Investigation Team

Compiling Report Location 97

Decision to be Made After Lytton and Others Inspect Qingdao

Japanese Side Opposes Beidaihe, with Hidden Intentions

Beijing Correspondence – The League of Nations investigation team held a routine meeting at the Beijing Hotel at 10:00 AM on the 7th to discuss everything. Around 10:00 AM, Secretary-General Haas and Secretary Wu Xiufeng went to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to begin sorting out documents. Regarding the location for writing the report, there was originally a proposal for Beidaihe. The Japanese side strongly opposed this, advocating for Qingdao or Xingpu in Dalian. The investigation team had no preconceived notions regarding the location, only that it should be quiet, cool, and suitable for work. To accommodate the Japanese request, it was decided to visit Qingdao for inspection before making a final decision. On the 7th, the team had already decided that Chairman Lytton would travel with the German representative Schnee, the Italian representative Marescotti, and one attendant. The remaining French representative Claudel, US representative McCoy, Secretary-General Haas, and other attendants would remain in Beijing to sort out the materials collected during the investigation. The Chinese side will be represented by Gu Weijun and attendants Liu Chongjie and Xiao Jirong, totaling three or four people. The Japanese side will be represented by Yoshida, Secretary Shiozaki, Colonel Kubota, and attendant Hayashi, departing from Beijing on the 8th at 6:00 PM after the Pingpu Railway resumes service, using three special cars. After arriving in Jinan, they will transfer to the Jiaoji Railway to Qingdao. It is reported that Lytton and others will only make a one-day inspection in Qingdao and return to Beijing on Friday. Gu Weijun plans to travel to Nanjing from Qingdao to report on the inspection of the Northeast and seek instructions on the future course of action.

Although Qingdao is located by the sea and the scenery is no less beautiful than Beidaihe, as a commercial port, the city is noisy, and with factories lining the streets and smoke billowing, it is far less quiet and suitable for work than Beidaihe. It is likely that Beidaihe will still be the main location in the future. On the 8th, after the routine meeting at 10:00 AM, the members of the investigation team went to their respective embassies for consultations. In the afternoon at 3:00 PM, the German representative visited the Summer Palace, while the French and Italian representatives visited the Temple of Heaven.

Furthermore, regarding the location for the investigation team to escape the heat and compile the report, according to informed sources, the final location for compiling the report is likely to be Qingdao. Initially, it was determined to be Beidaihe, but the Japanese side opposed this and advocated for Dalian, citing the reason that Beidaihe is under the sphere of influence of a certain party. However, the underlying reason is actually because Beidaihe is close to Shanhaiguan. Before the investigation team returned to Shenyang from northern Manchuria, the Japanese army in Yuguan frequently conducted exercises and provocative actions, and the situation was extremely dangerous for a time. When the investigation team passed through Yuguan, the Japanese side made every effort to conceal the situation to prevent them from discovering it. If the investigation team were to reside by the sea in the future, the actions of the Japanese army in Yuguan would be difficult to escape their eyes and ears. Moreover, residing by the sea for at least a month is a considerable amount of time, which is especially disliked by the Japanese side. However, the investigation team not only did not agree to Dalian, but also rejected the Japanese side's proposed Xingpu area between Dalian. Japan finally proposed Qingdao, and the team also favored this place. After touring Beidaihe, they stated that they intended to tour several more places before making a decision, but this was just to leave room for detailed consideration. Now that they are only going to Qingdao, there seems to be a kind of decision implicitly, and there is little doubt that the report will be drafted in Qingdao in the future. As for what the investigation team calls "inspection," it is probably just a kind of disguise to make both the Chinese and Japanese sides look good. (8th)

Cheng Zhiyuan

Atrocities in Heihe 98

Expanding Puppet Troops to Attack Righteous Army

Cheng's Defection Led to Brutal Harm

Sad Winds and Bitter Rain Fill Jiangcheng

Beijing Correspondence – According to people from Heihe, since Ma Zhanshan expressed his attitude, patriots and volunteer armies in various places have responded one after another. Li Haiqing led 20,000 volunteer soldiers on May 14th from Fuyu County, crossing the river to Qiqihar and the western section of the Chinese Eastern Railway line. The Japanese 15th Brigade, led by Amano, dispatched Cheng Zhiyuan's 8th Brigade, 54th Regiment, led by Regiment Commander Tu Quansheng, to resist. Cheng believed that attacking anti-Japanese elements everywhere would not be successful without adding troops. Amano, considering that Cheng was exceptionally devoted to the puppet state, was quite amenable to his suggestion and requested instructions from Honjo Shigeru. Honjo approved Cheng's temporary formation of two cavalry brigades. All clothing, arms, and ammunition were to be allocated by Liaoning. The Japanese side, fearing future disadvantages, ordered the recruitment of bandits, with officers jointly appointed by China and Japan. Honjo urgently telegraphed the Tokyo government, ordering all students from the Army University to come to Manchuria to await assignments. The president of the Army University, Ushijima, led all 58 students to Qiqihar on May 18th. Although Cheng Zhiyuan actively recruited new soldiers, no one responded. He again sent people to recruit bandits from various places, but only formed two regiments, which were combined with Tu Quansheng's 54th Regiment to form a brigade. At that time, Li

Page 10

Haiqing had occupied the Zhaodong area. The Japanese side appointed Tu Quansheng as the commander of the 2nd Cavalry Brigade and overall commander, with Zhu Fengyang's 55th Regiment of the 8th Brigade as support. Amano dispatched the 16th Regiment as a support team, and they advanced towards Zhaozhou. When the two armies faced off, soldiers on both sides fired into the air. After being threatened by Tu's collaborators and Japanese vehicles, Li Haiqing's soldiers shouted, "Japanese advance, Chinese retreat!", shaking the heavens and the earth. Tu and Zhu's regiments defected one after another. The Japanese army immediately launched fierce artillery fire and aircraft dropped bombs, causing an unprecedented fire in the Machang area of Zhaozhou County. Tu's accomplice had his right ring and little fingers completely blown off by Li's army artillery fire, and his left foot was blasted into a hole, rendering him disabled. He is currently recovering from his injuries in the provincial government hospital. Zhu's accomplice barely escaped with his life. As a result, Anda, Tiangegang, Duingshan, and Lanxi all fell within Li's army's area of influence. The Japanese side, realizing that Chinese-recruited bandits could not be effectively commanded, and that Japanese leadership would be even more unacceptable, sent the incoming Army University students back to Japan. On the 20th, the Cheng Zhiyuan guard machine gun company stationed at the Wufuma station on the Qi'ang Railway (18 li from the provincial capital) completely defected, responding to Li's army. The provincial capital was filled with rumors, and there were several alarms in one night. The Japanese army and Cheng's forces dispatched numerous detectives to investigate everywhere, arresting an uncountable number of people, falsely accusing and unjustly killing them. It is almost impossible to enumerate. After Cheng's treacherous killing of Ma Zhanshan's representative Wang Tinglan, he recently informed the Japanese military police on May 19th that Dai Shuqing, the office director of Ma Zhanshan's 3rd Cavalry Brigade stationed in Heihe, was secretly communicating with Chairman Ma, requesting their prompt arrest. The Japanese military police then arrested Dai and a driver surnamed Man, along with a wicker bag of documents. After interrogation, Man was released on bail. Dai was subjected to numerous severe tortures but ultimately did not confess. On the night of May 28th at 8:00 PM, the Japanese military police captain, Kaimura, suddenly summoned Dai, ordering him to write hundreds of characters in regular script. He was then imprisoned in a confinement room. At 1:00 AM that night, Dai was summoned again and his whereabouts became unknown. Two days later,

When Dai's servant went to inquire, the Japanese military police stated that he had been released on the 28th. On May 30th, Cheng Zhiyuan shot and killed two more officers from Ma's army, one being Wen Junfu, who served as the lieutenant colonel battalion commander in Deng's regiment (i.e., Deng Wen) under Chairman Ma, and the other being Liu Xiufeng, who served as the major company commander in the same battalion. They were ordered to go to the Yian County area. Wen and Liu remained composed, delivering impassioned speeches that were lamented by many. After the execution, the heavens and the earth took on a sorrowful appearance. Currently, the troops in Heilongjiang province who have submitted to Cheng include Xu Baozhen's brigade stationed in Sandaozhen, Baiquan County, Tu Quansheng's brigade stationed in the provincial capital, Pu BingShan's brigade stationed in Baiquan, and Cheng Zhiyuan's own 8th Brigade stationed in Taianzhen, up to the Daxing station area. The railway protection troops who have surrendered to Ma include Wu Songlin's brigade, Zhang Xiangge's brigade, Su Bingwen's brigade, and the volunteer army led by Li Haiqing, totaling about 45,000 people. Ma's troops have now retreated to Tongbei County, and Cai Hongyou has retreated to Qingcheng. Recently, rumors have spread throughout the provincial capital, and Cheng has intensified the search and arrest of anti-Japanese elements. The current situation in Heihe is almost one of sad winds and bitter rain filling Jiangcheng. Cheng Zhiyuan's troops, according to the Manchurian puppet army system, have three regiments per brigade, each regiment has three major companies, and each platoon has a fixed number of 18 people. The organization is now complete. The Japanese side, in order to raise funds, plans to establish an opium monopoly bureau, so poppies have been planted everywhere in Heilongjiang Province.

Liu Guitang

Leads Troops to Flee to Hebei 99

Han Sends Zhang and Chen's Brigades to Pursue

Jinan Correspondence - Liu Guitang (i.e., Liu Hei Qi)'s troops have long harassed southern Shandong, being the biggest scourge of Shandong. In 1928, when the National Revolutionary Army was on the Northern Expedition, Liu was commissioned as an army commander and participated in the battles. After the National Revolutionary Army recovered Shandong, Liu was stationed in the eastern Shandong area. Before long, he was ordered to transfer to Henan. Along the way, he extorted weapons from local militias and forcibly demanded loans, causing unbearable harassment to the people. The brigade was reorganized into the Northeastern Army's newly编旅, stationed in Daming, but still failed to abide by military discipline, harassing the local population. The central government then sent the 4th Division, led by Xu Tingyao, last year to resolve the situation. Liu again led his troops to break through the encirclement and fled into western Shandong, crossing the Yellow River from Feicheng Dawenkou, and returned to southern Shandong and eastern Shandong, capturing Rizhao, taking Zhucheng, and returning to his old nest in Feixian. Recently, through the introduction of Zhang Futian, he was incorporated by Han Fuju, with a total of over 3,000 troops and over 2,000 rifles. He was transferred to the Gaotang Yaodian area on the north bank of the Yellow River. After inspection and verification, he was reorganized into the Shandong Garrison Army, with Han himself serving as the commander-in-chief, Liu Guitang as the deputy commander and commander of the first route, and Guo Mafeng as the commander of the second route. The military pay and treatment were the same as those of the third route. Unexpectedly, Liu still considered it insufficient and continued to extort money from the local population. During this recent bandit suppression in northern Shandong, Liu was alarmed and drove away the county magistrate, and surrounded and disarmed the local militia. Upon receiving the report, Han immediately sent troops to surround them. Liu and Guo then led their troops to flee into Hebei province at 2:00 AM on the 8th, intending to go to northern Henan. The army is currently pursuing them. A detailed account of the situation is given below.

Bandit Uprising - Liu Guitang, seeing that the provincial army was successively being transferred to northern Shandong in large numbers, fearing that it would be detrimental to him, decided to strike first. On the morning of the 6th, he first sent troops to surround the Gaotang Public Security Bureau, forcing them to surrender their weapons. County Magistrate Zhang Kebao was driven out, and the city gates were tightly closed, leaving only two gates open to send off the families of the bandits. The people of Gaotang were extremely frightened and fled the city, supporting the old and carrying the young. The training officers and other personnel sent by the provincial government to Liu's troops were not harmed, but were disarmed and expelled. The office established by Liu at Wancheng Railway Station had over twenty cavalrymen. They were transferred back to Gaotang one night. Guo Mafeng led a portion of his troops to garrison Yaodian, and also gathered in Gaotang on the morning of the 7th, but did not enter the city, garrisoning the city corner to take a 角之勢.

Large-Scale Encirclement - Sun Tongxuan, the temporary commander-in-chief of the bandit suppression in northern Shandong, received an alarm about the Gaotang incident. He reported to the provincial government on the one hand and ordered the 85th Brigade, led by Li Hanzhang, stationed in Dezhou, to advance westward, and the 86th Brigade, led by Chen Dexin, stationed in Dongchang, to advance northeastward. Zhao Renquan's northern Shandong militia command was stationed in Linqing, responsible for the northern front, and the 58th Brigade, led by Zhang Shulin, stationed in Pingyuan,

Was on the eastern front, forming a large-scale encirclement of Gaotang and Yaodian. Commander-in-Chief Sun Tongxuan was stationed in Pingyuan, commanding everything. Li Shuchun, after inspecting Pingyuan, Dezhou, Yucheng, and Enxian, also arrived in Pingyuan to assist in the suppression. Chairman Han, because Gaotang was only 75 li from Yucheng Railway Station, fearing that the bandits would attack Yucheng Station and disrupt traffic, also sent the hand pistol brigade commander Lei Taiping, leading the special service battalion to garrison Yucheng to prevent any eventuality. Liu Guitang's office in Yucheng was disbanded by the armored car commander Dai Hongbin on the morning of the 6th. The office in Jinan was also disbanded by the garrison command. Office director Xu Peiyan fled upon hearing the news.

Nightly Alert - Currently, armored car commander Dai Hongbin leads the Beiping armored car on nightly patrol between Dezhou and Zhangzhuang. The 58th Brigade is on the front line, advancing westward from Pingyuan. The 20th Division's artillery unit also advanced from Pingyuan. Two companies of the 20th Division's cavalry advanced from Yucheng at 9:00 PM on the 6th, only 30 to 40 li from Gaotang. Yucheng, because it is closer to Gaotang, is under even stricter alert. At 6:00 PM in the afternoon, the city gates were closed, and the Taishan armored car, with two companies of special service soldiers, patrolled between Gaotang and Yucheng. The remaining two companies garrisoned Yucheng, and the night inspections were strict, with frequent password changes. The troops all bivouacked in the open.

Bandits Flee to Hebei - With the deployment of the various units completed, they advanced forward on the 7th. Liu Guitang and Guo Mafeng, seeing that the Gaotang city wall was low and the moat shallow, and unable to hold out, led their troops out of the west gate at 2:00 AM on the 8th and fled into Hebei province. Their purpose was to flee through Hebei province to Henan. One theory is that they intended to defect to Sun Dianying. Because the Gaotang Tongji long-distance telephone line was destroyed by them, the various parties received the report extremely late. Lei Taiping, after the bandits fled, returned to Jinan at 2:30 PM in the afternoon with the special service battalion on an armored car to report to Chairman Han Fuju.

Han Fuju Speaks - Provincial government chairman Han Fuju spoke about the incident, saying that Liu's troops fled southwest, apparently intending to flee to northern Henan. He had already ordered 58th Brigade Commander Zhang Shulin and 86th Brigade Commander Chen Dexin to track and pursue them, but the bandits were moving very quickly, and it was unknown whether they could catch up. Division Commander Sun and Commissioner Li had already arrived in Gaotang to handle the aftermath. It was not yet known what the losses were in Gaotang, and a report had not yet been received. He had also telegraphed

The troops stationed in northern Henan to jointly suppress them. It was also heard that Sun Tongxuan and Li Shuchun had already driven to Qingping to command the various armies to pursue the bandits. The Beiping armored car had already left Pingyuan and was waiting in Yucheng for orders.

Zhang's Bandits Flee, Southern Shandong Bandits Request Surrender - Over 1,000 troops of Zhang Heilian, Wang Changyou, and other notorious bandits in southern Shandong requested to surrender. Han Fuju sent Xia Ziming and Meng Guangshan to negotiate. Zhang, Wang, and others gathered at the Nanshahe Railway Station, outside the north gate on the 7th at 9:00 PM, planning to open and station in Yucheng.

Unexpectedly, upon arriving at Liangxiadian Railway Station south of Zou County, they received news of the solution of Liu Guitang and Guo Mafeng's troops. They immediately got off the train and fled, one part fleeing to the southwest of the railway in the Yanghu area, and the other part fleeing to the east of the railway back to their old nest. However, the government had made preparations in advance, so the 22nd Division Commander Gu Liangmin

Was responsible for pursuing those west of the railway, and the 81st Division Tang Bangzhi's brigade and the southern Shandong militia Xie Shushi's troops were responsible for pursuing those east of the railway, striving to take advantage of their fatigue to suppress them and eliminate the scourge for the people.

Issuing Complications - As for the personnel from Liu Guitang's office in Jinan and the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Army who were arrested in recent days, from Liu Guitang's side, a total of over 30 people were arrested in Jinan, and over 40 people were arrested in Yucheng and escorted to Jinan, including over ten women. On the afternoon of the 8th, Han Fuju interrogated them and immediately released over twenty innocent suspects. The over ten women were also ordered to be taken back by their families after it was confirmed that they were good people. As for the remaining prisoners, they were temporarily detained. Also, there was a son of Xia Ziming, whom Han told that there was no danger and that he did not need to be afraid, but that he would temporarily be handed over to Public Security Bureau Chief Wang Kairu for preferential detention to prevent contact with the outside. Also, one army commander, division commanders, brigade commanders, and quartermasters of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Army, totaling over ten people, all confessed that they were appointed by Fu Cunhuai and others from Yan Xishan's side. Han then ordered them to be temporarily detained for investigation before interrogation. (8th)

Jiading 102

Relief for Disaster Victims: Building Memorial Villages The Shanghai Municipal Local Maintenance Association, in response to the destruction of 2,618 houses in this county by the Japanese army, and the resulting destitution and temporary shelter arrangements of many disaster victims, has allocated 35,000 yuan specifically for the construction of memorial villages in the affected areas, to provide housing for the disaster victims. On the 9th, Yang Weiyu was dispatched to Jiading to meet with the county's relief sub-committee to discuss implementation measures. Wuxi 103

Continuous Occurrence of Robbery Cases in Urban and Rural Areas In Wuxi, within the recent half-month, in addition to the continuous occurrence of rice looting incidents in the four rural districts, murder and robbery cases have also occurred almost daily. On the 1st of last month, two more cases occurred, as described below: (1) At the Yi Sheng Chun timber business located at Gengdu Bridge outside the South Gate, five robbers suddenly arrived at 9:00 PM on the 9th, carrying four pistols. One of the robbers, acting as the leader, entered the accounting room directly, declaring, "We have five boats passing through your area and need 400 yuan to boost our morale." While he spoke, another robber climbed upstairs and cut the electric light wires, commencing a thorough search and robbery, lasting half an hour before leaving with the loot. The result was the robbery of approximately one hundred yuan in silver coins and paper money, as well as a large quantity of clothing. (2) In the Chao Yin Qing Zhou Pi Jiang Ba area of the Second District, residents Zhou Hongsheng, Hongshun, and Hongmao, three brothers, lived together in one house, occupying the upper and lower floors. They typically farmed and also worked as rice boatmen, and had therefore accumulated some savings. At 12:00 AM the previous night, more than ten robbers suddenly broke into the house, splitting up to search the three households. When they arrived at Hongsheng's room, Hongsheng, recently having planned for self-defense, had prepared a rifle and a pistol, both with permits. One robber first grabbed the pistol from beside his pillow, along with seven bullets, jumped onto the table, and directed the other robbers in their search. He also took out an account book from his pocket and flipped through the pages. Hongsheng, curled up in a corner of the room, secretly observed that nearly thirty households in the entire village with some wealth were listed in the account book. After an hour, they left with the loot towards Qianqiao. Before leaving, they fired shots continuously as a show of force. After inspection, the three households had lost more than one thousand yuan in total, and Hongmao's wife, Wu, was also severely injured with a sharp blade.

The Seventh District Resolves to Provide Relief and Self-Defense Zhao Yingqiu, the head of the Seventh District, recently convened the township heads due to the continuous occurrence of rice looting incidents in the district. Unscrupulous elements have taken the opportunity to become active, and public safety in the rural areas is in imminent danger. He convened the township heads to organize a relief committee and resolved the following: (1) Relief for impoverished farmers will be divided into three categories: concessional loans, price stabilization, and porridge distribution. Village leaders and neighbors will conduct thorough investigations, allocating loans to the poorest, price-stabilized grain to the next poorest, and porridge to the most impoverished. (2) Relief funds will be raised by each township from wealthy residents, rich households, granaries, charitable estates, and wealthy gentlemen in other ports. (3) Each township will organize a temporary defense corps or watch post within a specified timeframe to assist existing self-defense organizations in protecting the local area. (4) If any unscrupulous elements are found in any township, they will be reported to the county government for investigation and punishment according to the law. (5) The townships will report the implementation of the relief and self-defense measures to the county government for record.

The 19th Route Army Volunteer Corps Holds Graduation Ceremony The 19th Route Army's 78th Division, 156th Brigade Volunteer Corps, the 1st, 2nd, and 3rd Battalions, and the officer training class, totaling over 800 students, bravely fought the enemy during the January 28th Shanghai Incident and achieved significant merit. Since the Sino-Japanese armistice, the army has been under the training of Brigade Commander Weng for two months. Yesterday (the 10th) was the end of the army's training period. A graduation ceremony was held at the Sheqiao Provincial People's Education College's parade ground in this county. Army Commander Cai Tingkai arrived in Wuxi from Suzhou at 12:45 PM. Local leaders and officials stationed in Wuxi went to the station to welcome him. Representatives from the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and other organizations also came to Wuxi to participate. The meeting began at 1:00 PM, presided over by District Commander (Shounian), with customary ceremonies. Army Commander Cai Tingkai gave a speech, briefly stating that after graduation, everyone should continue to strive in their studies. The 60th Division Commander Shen Guanghan spoke, stating that after graduation, everyone must still bear the responsibility of saving the nation. Finally, District Commander (Shounian) spoke, stating that after graduation, he hoped everyone would continue to save the nation and resist foreign aggression. Zhao Yijian and others then delivered speeches, and graduation certificates were distributed. Photos were taken and the ceremony adjourned.

Fish Business Inspection Causes Great Disturbance Zhao Yuting, the Chief Inspector of the Public Security Bureau, reported on the evening of the 7th around 7:00 PM that someone was smoking opium at the Zengshun fish business west of Puhui Bridge outside the North Gate. Jiaxing 107

Silk Filature Taxes Have Been Approved for Exemption Due to various factors, silk merchants in Jiaxing are unwilling to establish filatures to purchase cocoons this silkworm season. The Silk Industry Association, to facilitate farmers' sale of cocoons, repeatedly urged silk merchants to raise funds to open filatures to purchase cocoons. However, due to economic reasons, less than one-tenth of the silk filatures in the county have opened. The association also requested the relevant ministries and provincial authorities to exempt all taxes and surcharges to alleviate the difficulties faced by the merchants due to poor silkworm harvests. It is now learned that the Ministry of Finance, after reviewing the request, believes that the situation presented is indeed factual and has instructed the Zhejiang Provincial Government to order the Departments of Finance and Construction to approve the exemption of silk filature taxes and surcharges for one year. The association has been notified accordingly.

Important News

The Storm at Peiping University Escalates 108

Strike Picketers Seal Off Classrooms

The Ministry of Education Will Send Representatives to Mediate

Peiping, 10th The Joint Association of Schools and Colleges of Peiping University (平大) informed the press this morning that if Shen Yinmo does not resign, they are determined to use force to remove him. The Normal University went on strike this morning, and picketers sealed off all classrooms, declared martial law, and prohibited entry and exit, preparing to go to Beijing to demand the president's removal.

From Beijing sources In recent days, the Ministry of Education has received a deluge of telegrams from students of eight schools requesting the removal of presidents and deans. Considering that this matter has a significant impact on the future of education in Peiping and Tianjin, and that the authorities cannot shirk their responsibility if the storm unfortunately escalates, the Ministry of Education plans to send representatives to Peiping within days to mediate and investigate the cause of the incident in order to resolve it. Peiping, 10th Three thousand students from various schools and colleges of Peiping University plan to surround Peiping University on the 11th. After receiving the news, Yinmo telegraphed the Ministry of Education to resign and will not go to school from the 11th.

Entire Faculty of Zhejiang University

Resolves Leave-Taking Crisis 109

|Classes Suspended for One Day with One Month's Salary Paid

|Classes Resumed Normally on the 9th

The entire faculty of the Colleges of Engineering, Agriculture, Liberal Arts, and Sciences of Zhejiang University had been in arrears of salary for three months, with only payments up to the end of February made. In light of the increasing cost of living, they felt unable to maintain their livelihoods. Representatives from the Colleges of Engineering, Agriculture, and Liberal Arts had repeatedly urged the university to issue the arrears, but to no avail. Therefore, an emergency meeting of the entire faculty was convened, and it was resolved to take collective leave starting from the 8th. Consequently, all three colleges simultaneously suspended classes. President Cheng Tianfang was in Nanjing negotiating for funds. The university authorities, in addition to immediately telegraphing Cheng to return to Hangzhou as soon as possible, made every effort to raise funds. On the same evening, they issued one month's salary for March to the entire faculty of the three colleges, totaling over 40,000 yuan, requesting them to resume classes as usual. The entire faculty of the university also resumed classes on the 9th due to student academic concerns, thus resolving the collective leave-taking crisis.

Dean of Engineering College of Zhejiang University Resigns 110

Li Ximou, the Dean of the College of Engineering of Zhejiang University, has been in office since 1927, a period of five years. Last year, due to the petition of the College of Engineering's student volunteer army, which led to the destruction of the provincial party headquarters and the residence of Zhang Daofan, the magistrate of the education county, he once resigned to take responsibility. Unexpectedly, he has recently become dissatisfied with the students, who issued an anti-Li declaration. Li then submitted his resignation to Cheng Tianfang, the president of Zhejiang University, instructing the heads of departments to handle the handover. He has not been to school since the 8th, and his resignation is resolute, expressing that he is unwilling to return to office. The students of the college convened an emergency general meeting the night before last, unanimously resolving that there was no need to retain Li's resignation and deciding on the criteria for the new dean: (1) high moral character, (2) profound knowledge, (3) a respected figure in the industrial sector, (4) no political affiliations.

Draft of Vocational School Organization Law by the Ministry of Education

The Ministry of Education passed the draft of the Vocational School Organization Law, consisting of nineteen articles, at the Ministry Affairs Conference and Symposium on the 8th. It will be formally promulgated after going through the necessary procedures. The main points of the draft, as decided by public discussion on that day, are extracted below: (1) Vocational schools aim to impart knowledge to young people to enable them to live independently, enhance their skills in production and labor, and cultivate their morality of serving society. (2) Two levels will be established: junior and senior. Junior vocational schools will specialize in one type of skill depending on local needs. When necessary, several vocational departments may be established to train skilled workers. Senior vocational schools will establish various specialized departments with higher standards, depending on local needs, to train skilled technicians or management personnel in various industries. (3) Senior vocational schools will be established by the province or municipalities directly under the Executive Yuan in principle. Junior vocational schools may be established by industrial and commercial organizations or industrial institutions and private individuals. The county and municipal governments should supervise or jointly establish them with industrial and commercial organizations or industrial institutions in principle, and the county and municipal governments may provide appropriate subsidies. When necessary, they may be established by the county and municipal governments or jointly established by two or more counties. (4) Vocational schools at all levels may establish various supplementary classes as appropriate. (5) Junior vocational schools should, in principle, not charge tuition fees.

This order."

Local News

National Jinan University President Zheng Departs for Guangdong Today 112

Concluding the University Department in Guangdong and Preparing for the Establishment of a Middle School Department

Returning to Shanghai in Two Weeks

National Jinan University has suffered enormous losses since the Shanghai Incident. President Zheng and all the faculty and staff have worked tirelessly and spared no effort to continue the school by borrowing temporary school buildings in Shanghai in the shortest possible time. On the one hand, it has established a university department in Guangzhou, and on the other hand, it has established a middle school department in Suzhou, so that students scattered throughout the country can continue their studies. Now that the school has undergone this war, it has decided to take the opportunity to improve the school. A post-war reorganization committee has been established a few days ago to conduct careful research on future reform plans. Recently, the school affairs meeting of the school decided that starting from the next semester, the middle school department will be established in Guangzhou, and the normal school department will be established separately in Suzhou, with an affiliated experimental school, which is specially designed for students who are interested in education in the department and various departments of the university department. As for the Zhenru school building, it will be completely used as the university department. The university department stationed in Guangdong will be revoked at the end of this semester and moved back to Zhenru. The principal of the school, in order to end the university department in Guangzhou and prepare for the establishment of a middle school department, will personally return to Guangdong to plan everything, and will take the Coolidge mail ship south today, and it is expected that he will stay there for two weeks.

Temporary Bureau Affairs Meeting of the County Education Bureau 113

The Shanghai County Education Bureau held a temporary bureau affairs meeting yesterday morning, attended by Director Shi, Superintendent Zhu, Zheng Guozhai, Yang Huiming, Lin Weiwen, Niu Zhiyi, Shen Jingzhi, and Zheng Shaoyuan. Liu Yunshu was present, Director Shi chaired the meeting, and Pan Shengsan took the minutes. After the customary ceremonies, the following items were discussed: (1) How should the service methods for the current county-run rural normal school graduates be stipulated? It was resolved to stipulate as follows: (A) Selection criteria: those with excellent grades and suitable for the location. (B) Selection method: The education committee members and principals of each elementary school must first report any teaching vacancies and be sent by the bureau to serve. (C) Service period: limited to one semester, and may not be interrupted. (D) Living expenses: a discretionary allowance of 15 yuan per month. (2) In accordance with the order, the rent for February and March of this year will be reduced, and the deadline for rent payment will be set. It was resolved to set the deadline as June 20.

Sports

Grass Society Mixed Doubles Opening Match

Ancient Temple Bell Recordings (10) (9) 114

Not Removing the Courtyard Grass

Twenty-one

Mr. Zhu was as strange as we were. He didn't ask us how much tuition we gave him each month, nor did he ask us how many hours of lessons we wanted him to teach each day. What was the reason for this? Could it be that he was a wealthy man who didn't want to fuss about salary and hours? Why weren't these salary and hour issues a problem in his mind? Could it be that he was so happy to have found a place where he could assert his own ideas that he forgot about these problems? Who knows? ···········

Two people carrying two loads gradually approached. Who? Wasn't that tall man Mr. Zhu? The smaller one must be his younger brother. The teacher himself was carrying bedding! This was the first time I had ever seen such a thing in my life. ······ Mr.! Why are you carrying your own luggage? This is exactly our opportunity to serve you. ······· Brother Chunsheng! You carry for the little brother, and I'll carry for the teacher, okay?” I volunteered. Brother Chunsheng ran up to snatch the teacher's larger luggage, and said to me, "You are younger, you should carry the smaller one."

Who knew that Mr. Shi was determined to carry his own bedding to the countryside. No matter what we said, he refused to let us carry it. His reason was quite simple. He said: "This is the first lesson I learned from you. Country people carry firewood into the city to sell, and we should follow their example." But how could we agree with him? He was our newly hired teacher. How could we just stand by with our hands empty and comfortably watch the teacher sweat? In the end, Old Madam Song proposed a compromise: the four of us would take turns carrying the two loads of luggage. However, when we got close to the ancient temple, we had to let Brother Chunsheng and Zhonger carry it. Old Madam Song's suggestion was accepted by both sides. After all, the teacher's shoulders were very tender, and the younger brother's were even more tender. When we got to the ancient temple and took off our clothes, we saw that our shoulders were as red as if we had been scratched, and two fleshy bumps had grown up. The younger brother said later that he felt particularly sore all night. He thought it was very interesting to carry the load to the countryside this time. He said that he would never look down on those who carried loads again, because he had carried them himself and knew that he could only take one step by putting in one ounce of effort. How adorable this little brother was!

Twenty-two

It is needless to say that country people make jokes when they come to town. Who knew that city people would make jokes when they went to the countryside? Our lovely little brother made no fewer jokes than I did. Let's just talk about one thing. When we walked to the gate of the temple, the little brother pointed to the green fields in front of the temple and said, "How can you eat so much chives that you grow?" This sentence caused everyone to burst into laughter, and the naive little brother was stunned. He didn't know why everyone was laughing. Old Madam Song was quick to say, "This is wheat seedlings, not chives. Do you like to eat chives?" The little brother himself laughed with a red face. Mr. Zhu said, "I've said it before, there are many things you can teach us." Little brother! How happy you are. Old Madam Song taught you what wheat is. You have to carefully compare the wheat seedlings with the chives to find out exactly what the difference is. In the future, as long as you ask people modestly, you will be able to make progress every day. As for things you don't know, you should be brave enough to ask questions, and be shy about talking nonsense."

Shanghai's Educational Undertakings After the January 28th Incident (10) (4) Still 115

Twenty-one Post-War Matters

In the 20th century, among the nations of the world, who can find a second race as unpromising as the race in this country? The countries that have fallen have long been working hard to turn over and carry out their vigorous recovery plans, but we are languid and depressed, losing power and humiliating ourselves, spreading ugliness to the world, adding shame to shame, disaster to disaster, piling up firewood under the house, snoring outside, the superiors are still living in luxury and comfort as if nothing happened, and the inferiors are still playing and enjoying themselves in the danger of being slaughtered, and the great disaster is one step closer and one step pressing, and has entered the hall and reached the chamber. The September 18th Incident in Northeast China has not yet ended, and then the great disaster of the January 28th Incident has come to Shanghai, the most prosperous area near the capital, such a heart-wrenching and humiliating event, I don't know if it can awaken the good dreams of officials and people in general, if they wake up from a dream, they may suddenly understand the state of their debts, the sun and the moon, the mountains and rivers are the same, how different are the past and the present? Where is the former prosperity now? Where are the former fields now? What is left of the former culture now? The ancestors painstakingly created, the reputation of history, and we ourselves cut it off, how can we not feel ashamed, not to mention only ashamed?

The resistance of the 19th Route Army and the 5th Army for 34 days, sacrificing the blood and flesh of thousands of martyrs and destroying the lives and property of tens of thousands of civilians, only resulted in a ceasefire agreement. The takeover committee of the withdrawal area was actually established. However, the enemy troops temporarily bid farewell, who can guarantee that there will be no future troubles? If they are foolish and selfish, and do not strengthen themselves, then what is the use of signing thousands of agreements? Treating the head when it hurts, treating the feet when they hurt, what is the point of the method of neither dying nor living? Relying on the treaty, the enemy, whose army has not withdrawn, can use it as coercion and threat at any time and anywhere. The poem says "When the sky is just beginning, do not let it leak," Gongzi said, "Walking on frost is colder than walking on solid ice, birds in the rain are more worried than birds in the wind, numbness is worse than ulcers, and withered flowers are more miserable than dead wood." The country has not fallen, but the pain is worse than the fall of the country. The Songhu war zone has not been lost, but the disaster is more severe than the loss of land. Compatriots, compatriots, do not forget that when the news of the takeover of the war zone comes, the joy of restoring the highest power is buried with endless hidden worries.

Under deep pain, mourning like losing parents is useless, blood vessels bursting and hair standing on end is useless, bowing heads and stretching eyebrows, and speaking frankly is even more useless, only by thinking about the pain and exploring the past, and striving for the future, can we heal the wounds and restore vitality, "Everything that can be destroyed by human power can also be restored by human power," this is a Western saying, I hope the people of the country remember it, even if the war zone is ashes, as long as the people do not become sand worms, and the government does not become foolish, constantly inspiring and encouraging each other, creating new material resources, and laying a solid new foundation, then the educational undertakings in the war zone will not be difficult to restore to their original state, and it will not be difficult to develop and grow. If we are not a nation that is about to perish, if we are a nation with ambition, then with the flesh and blood and white bones of the heroic martyrs who defended the country as the raw materials for the development of Shanghai, the future culture will be more difficult to promote and develop, "A virtuous person can govern the country, only in times of great difficulty can the country be prosperous." Compatriots, compatriots, this is an opportunity to awaken us, this is the driving force for innovation and self-improvement, only with hard work can we reap a thriving harvest, now let's talk about the cultivation of educational undertakings after taking over the territory.

The post-war measures for educational undertakings in the war zone should be divided into two major steps: symptomatic treatment and fundamental treatment, and the government and the people should make efforts in both directions. First, let's talk about the problem of symptomatic treatment.

(1) Symptomatic treatment The first thing after taking over Shanghai, the reporter feels that there is no need to rush to the construction of education, I have heard that in the Japanese earthquake in September of the 12th year of Taisho, Tokyo lost a total of 1.4 billion yuan, they erected temporary school buildings of white wood in the ruins and broken walls, and engaged in educating children. Six years after the disaster, the Kyoto Reconstruction Bureau did not start work on the government and its affiliated organs, but only on 117 elementary schools that stood tall in the sky. The construction cost of each school was more than 1.5 million Japanese gold, and the number of schools was more than before the earthquake, this seems to be a good material worth referring to for today's authorities, the reporter's opinion is that the current government should urgently hire experts and enthusiastic educators to set up a "War Zone Education Rehabilitation Committee" to plan the rehabilitation of education affairs, after the war zone is restored, the government can first start investigating, all facilities, should be based on the results of the investigation as a basis, the investigation should focus on whether the transportation is convenient, whether the population is large, whether the school-age children are gathered, if the above conditions require a school, then immediately set up a "temporary primary school", the standard for setting up a temporary primary school is not whether there is a school building, but the number of students, if there are 30 school-age children in a certain area, then a single-grade temporary primary school can be set up, and the current unemployed teachers can be used to fill the position, extend the daily teaching time, attend classes as usual on Sundays, stop putting on the summer vacation, make up for a semester's study, use time and space in the evening to enroll out-of-school adults, the poor are exempt from fees and given books and stationery, so that people who are out of school are proud to come to school, and those who are studying are persuaded to study hard, so as not to make those who have been educated sit and be idle, and those who have not been educated drop out of school for a long time, there are not many public secondary schools, and there are nine private secondary schools in Zhabei and five in Jiangwan that have been registered, and all classes are now taught elsewhere, it is certainly good to return to the original site this semester, and those who are not strong enough have to postpone their return to their hometown, fortunately, the middle school students are a little afraid of the years, and it is convenient to go to school and stay, schools with higher education buildings that have not been destroyed seem to be able to return early, so as to make full use of the good facilities, The principal is to end the University Department in Guangzhou and prepare for the establishment of a Middle School Department, and will personally return to Guangdong to plan everything, and will take the Coolidge mail ship south today, and it is expected that he will stay there for two weeks.

World Olympic Games Track and Field

Japan Not Permitted to Be Optimistic 120

First-Rate Performances Show Signs of Decline

Newcomers Lack Sufficient Confidence

Economic Impact Reduces Delegation Size

Germany Sends Only Nineteen Men and Women

For the World Olympic Games to be held in Los Angeles this autumn, the Japanese delegation has already decided to send 26 male and 9 female athletes, with Hiroshi Hasumi, Koichi Oyama, Toru Takada, and Yoshio Oki taking on the roles of instructors. According to observers familiar with the Japanese sports scene, it is difficult to predict the extent to which the Japanese track and field team will be able to perform this time, based on information from various sources. The reason is that in this spring's Olympic regional preliminaries in Japan and in the athletic leagues of universities and vocational schools, the once invincible Oda, Nakajima, Ichida, Kimura, Oshima and other athletes have encountered various obstacles. Although newcomers still possess the spirit of the old guard and are working extraordinarily hard, the date of the games is fast approaching. The Japanese plan to have those with rich experience at the forefront, with energetic newcomers as support, but those who could be alone are showing signs of decline, and the newcomers lack sufficient confidence, so it is difficult to be optimistic about the competitive prospects. Furthermore, due to economic factors, various European countries are also not enthusiastically sending athletes this year. For example, Germany is only sending 12 men and 7 women, indicating that in addition to sending elite athletes to participate in the upcoming Olympics, many countries also have a few first-rate individuals who are quietly observing the future success or failure within their own countries.

It is now known that the school has scheduled its sports day to be held on the school's sports field on the 18th of this month. Participants in track and field events account for one-third of the school's students, totaling more than 400 people. In addition, there will be group performances, and students' parents and sports figures will be invited to attend and observe.

Actually Opens a Historically Unprecedented Record

Market Overview: The intensity of this time's currency depreciation is truly unprecedented to us. Although the market's buying and selling are brave, it is probably because each individual's vision is different, and the truth is that there is no certainty about the practical future. According to yesterday's total decline of more than four candareens in both markets, it was indeed the first loud sound after entering the 7 candareen mark, but anticipating that such a loud sound will become familiar thereafter, one cannot help but be afraid.

Tianjin City

Recent News of the Disastrous Fall in West River Cotton Prices 131

Large Inventory, Low Sales, Good New Production

Lowest Peak Since the Third Year of the Republic at 18 Taels

Tianjin, 6th dispatch: Recently, the market price of West River cotton has plummeted, a rare occurrence in recent years. On June 1st, the price was 27 taels, but yesterday it reached a low of 23 taels and 5 qian. Enquiries made to fellow traders reveal that the decline in cotton prices this year is an undeniable fact. The recent sharp drop is due to: firstly, the holiday season is approaching, and Japanese merchants are taking a wait-and-see attitude, with little purchasing activity; secondly, general cotton merchants, seeing abundant rainfall this year, anticipate a good autumn harvest, and also because many Tianjin-produced cotton bales have failed inspection, cotton merchants urgently needing funds are impatiently selling off their stock. Moreover, spinning mills reportedly have enough inventory for two months of use, so one European merchant is inactive. Although it is impossible to predict how far the market price will fall, observations suggest this is the lowest price in the past fifteen years. In the third year of the Republic, the lowest price was 18 or 19 taels, but it soon returned to its former level. This year, the lowest price may reach the 20-tael mark. If furs and other goods become stagnant, it will be difficult to see a significant price drop, as Japanese merchants still have purchasing power, and spinning mills also have significant usage, so cotton demand should be substantial. Moreover, the impact of this price drop is not as great as last year's, when cotton prices rose and fell sharply, dropping from over 40 taels to below 30 taels, catching people off guard. Therefore, cotton brokers, warehouses, and money houses all suffered considerable losses.

After this price drop, the amount of losses is said to be around 1.6 million. Customers who stockpiled and provided funds are sharing this loss. Fortunately, most customers are creditworthy, so there have been no reports of bankruptcies. As for the cotton inventory in Tianjin, it currently remains around 145,000 bales, it is said.

Silk and Tea

Changshu Cocoon Production Reaching Its End 132

Overall Harvest Not Even 20%: Quality Lower

Changshu, the spring silkworms in the four suburban villages initially suffered from the military influence, and the number of people raising them was less than 40% of last year. Then, due to unfavorable weather and widespread silkworm diseases, many early silkworms lost their leaves. Although some late silkworms were raised in the Pengjiaqiao area, cocoon production was extremely poor, almost reaching its end, with the overall harvest not even 20%. The quality of the cocoons was lower than last year. Very few cocoon markets have opened. Silkworm farmers have cocoons but nowhere to sell them. Cocoon prices are only opening at 15 or 16 yuan, and they are all being dried in earthen stoves, it is said.

Flour Manufacturers Dumping Stock 136

Prices Plunging Over 4 Fen Each Month

Yesterday's flour market: after opening in the morning, prices for each month were initially stable, but because foreign wheat prices fell by another jiao or so (Chicago recently fell to around 4 jiao 9 fen), and because actual sales were sluggish, manufacturers, despite wanting to hold on to their chips, were unable to resist the fact that various grains were all falling, so flour prices were unlikely to be bullish. Given this situation, buyers were scarce, and the market situation softened again. By the time the market opened in the afternoon, the market atmosphere suddenly plunged wildly. Because a certain manufacturer slightly dumped stock, and the number of buyers decreased even more, the supply and demand gap widened, and a price drop was inevitable. The lowest price for July reached 8 qian, 6 fen, 7 li and a half, and the price for August reached 8 qian, 6 fen and a half, a difference of 5 fen from the closing price of the previous day. However, the closing price rose slightly, perhaps as a last hurrah. As a result, July fell by 3 fen and 7 li and a half compared to the previous day, August fell by 4 fen and 2 li and a half, September fell by 3 fen and 2 li and a half, October fell by 3 fen and 7 li and a half, and November fell by 3 fen and a half.

Wheat Futures Market Weakening Again 137

Yesterday's wheat futures market: after opening in the morning, the market for each month remained sluggish, and trading was also sparse. By the time the market opened in the afternoon, trading was smoother, but the market atmosphere weakened again and again because it is currently the peak season for new wheat to gradually enter the market, and manufacturers in this port have traditionally set up warehouses in the interior to purchase wheat, but this year they have no need for it because of the abundant supply of flour recently. This adverse environment is difficult to reverse in the short term (the quoted price for silver-top wheat is only 5 yuan, 3 jiao and 4 fen), so when sellers become active, the market atmosphere cannot avoid a setback. As a result, July fell by 5 fen compared to the previous day, August and September fell by 6 fen, October fell by 5 fen, and November fell by 4 fen, it is said.

Taikoo sugar from Tianjin was 16 taels and 2 qian, original goods were 16 taels and 4 qian, CW mark was 15 taels and 9 qian, H mark was 12 taels and 5 qian, and there were slight transactions. Taikoo spot H mark opened at 500 bags, priced at 6 taels and 5 qian, new regulations and taxes for CW mark are priced at 7 taels and 3 qian and a half, also new regulations including taxes, and the marked price is 16 taels and 1 quan, so the need for firms is scarce. The brokerage plate had Hua Xin Co. selling 300 bags of spot raw sugar, priced at 14 taels, and the market was also stable and not unusual, it is said.

Coal: Hard to Improve the Market Prices for White Coal 139

Recently, the sales of white coal have gradually become more active because customers from the Su and Hangzhou regions have slightly purchased some, but merchants in this port have purchased very little, so the selling price is difficult to improve. Yesterday's market saw 270 tons of Maike white coal traded at a price of 20 taels and 3 qian, 316 tons of Liujiang white coal at a price of 16 taels, 94 tons of Haifeng white coal at a price of 20 taels and 8 qian and a half, and 80 tons of Great Wall white coal at a price of 16 taels and 7 qian and a half. Also, Open Pit No. 1 Slag is currently selling for 9 taels and 1 qian per ton.

Hardware: New Iron Wire Arrivals, Brisk Sales Stagnating 140

The market for new iron wire had previously been trending well because the market was depleted and various merchants were eagerly buying, so the standard rose frequently. For example, sizes 16 to 20 were selling for 13 taels and a half per picul, and sizes 21 to 25 were selling for 14 taels and a half. However, in the past few days, goods have been arriving from various regions one after another, so that the market is flooded, people's confidence is declining, the standard opening price is gradually moving downstream, and the way out is even more sluggish and stagnant. Yesterday, more than 100 piculs were opened, with sizes 16 to 20 selling for 13 taels and sizes 21 to 25 selling for 14 taels, it is said.

Free Talk

Old Man Ma Xiangbo, Ninety-Three Years Old

Only Know How to Imitate the Past, Don't Know How to Seek Progress 141

— Nine

The underdevelopment of Chinese crafts is due to the lack of improvement in machinery and tools. "If a craftsman wants to do his job well, he must first sharpen his tools," is an old Chinese saying. But in the Chinese view, things made with sharp tools are not considered anything special. Only working with outdated, clumsy tools is considered Chinese skill. For example, in writing, instead of using a good writing brush, people use chicken feathers, fingernails, or write with a brush held in the mouth, and that is considered art.

Truly, national governance and doctrine are nothing more than guiding the creation of wealth and meeting needs, while safeguarding their freedom. Guiding requires reason, and safeguarding with property rights enables those who are able to persevere. Old Man Ma Xiangbo, Ninety-Three Years Old.

Chinese painting has also made very little progress. Paintings with perspective are considered the work of lowly craftsmen by Chinese connoisseurs. The Chinese only focus on writing, putting all their artistic spirit into it. Foreign alphabets have only twenty-odd letters and cannot be used as decorations, so foreigners cannot consider good handwriting as art. Only in China can one make money by writing for guests.

Foreign letters were created by monks, initially kept secret, and used as a monopoly by monks before being made public. I suspect that the origin of Chinese characters is similar. In fact, handwriting from three or four hundred years ago is not necessarily good, but a group of scholars with nothing to do come up with many tricks, imitating inscriptions from stone tablets. It is clear that the stone tablet is old, the writing is blurred, a stroke is missing, or a dot is missing, but copying it exactly is considered a good style. I think Wang Xizhi wrote cursive script when he was drunk, and even he himself did not recognize it, but later generations competed to copy it, and that is considered a style. So, writing also began to talk about systems and schools. So-and-so writes in the Han style, so-and-so writes in the Northern Wei style, so-and-so writes in the Yan style, so-and-so writes in the Su style, resulting in a variety of styles, and people do not put effort into art, but quarrel over schools. This is like guaranteeing a patron, not asking about ability, but asking who his teacher is.

Not only is writing like this, but so is writing. After the Tang and Song dynasties, there can be said to be no good writing, because everyone competes to establish their own schools, sticks to the old ways, and does not seek progress. What Yang Xiong style, Sima Qian's writing style, Han prose, Su prose, and so on. Everyone only knows how to imitate the past, and does not know how to seek progress. Zhang Taiyan is well-read in the Book of Han and even considers the broken styles of the ancients as ancient styles.

Continued Anecdotes of Resisting Aggression 142

— Iron Amitabha

I have already written anecdotes of resisting aggression. Now I have heard more and am writing a continuation.

Mr. He told me. Mr. He lives in Zhabei. On the night of January 28th of this year, he heard the start of the incident. Then the sound of gunfire and artillery gradually approached. Mr. He, curious and forgetful of the danger, crawled to the back of the house and peeked from beside the iron gate pillar. Suddenly, he saw our army retreating, abandoning several soldiers on the road, who looked severely wounded. Just as he was sighing, the enemy's tank had already approached, nearing the abandoned soldiers. The abandoned soldiers suddenly leaped up, each holding a gunpowder canister, and pounced on the enemy tank. A thunderous explosion sounded, accompanied by the enemy soldiers' cries of agony. Mr. He was extremely frightened and fled back. After a while, he only heard the shouts of our army resounding in all directions, and no longer heard the rumble of the tank. (Note: This is the first time the enemy was heavily defeated on Qiujiang Road, as reported in the news. The details were not clear, but now this account supplements the historical omission.)

Also, Mr. Zhao told me that on the night of February 7th, the enemy attacked a certain road. At that time, only three soldiers of our army were guarding this road. Two soldiers were taking a short rest in a house, leaving one soldier, Mr. Mou, on guard. Many enemies were attacking. Bullets rained down, but Mr. Mou did not take it seriously. He rushed to the front barricade, put his helmet on the gun, raised it above the barricade, and moved it left and right, making it seem like there were dozens of people. The enemy saw it in the firelight and immediately fired their guns. Mr. Mou also fired his machine gun intermittently in response. The Japanese knew they were prepared and fired even more densely. Mr. Mou thought the enemy would not dare to approach suddenly, so he ran back to call the resting soldiers. Reinforcements also arrived. The Japanese had not heard the sound of our army for a long time and thought they had fled, so they advanced to attack. Our army suddenly rose up and surrounded them, completely wiping out their entire army.

Also, Mr. Yun told me that a Cantonese man named Mr. Chen was skilled in shooting. One night, he and five or six other soldiers were guarding a certain pass at the North Railway Station. The enemy army attacked with more than thirty men, and their momentum was very fierce. The other soldiers were all worried about their safety. Mr. Chen smiled and said, "Watch me kill these fellows for you." Then they fired several shots and immediately ran to hide behind the barricade more than ten zhang away. The enemy knew they were prepared and attacked even more fiercely. Mr. Chen held his breath and did not respond, holding his machine gun and hiding under the barricade. After a while, the enemy thought they had fled and crossed the barricade to advance. Mr. Chen waited until they were between the barricade and the hiding place, suddenly rose up and attacked them. The hiding soldiers also rose up in response. The enemy, in the darkness and in a hurry, thought that a large army had arrived, and all abandoned their guns and fled, losing more than ten men. The five or six soldiers were unharmed.

World Anecdotes 143

— Sea Guest

Model Servants: Model servants refer to British servants. During America's golden age, many wealthy people traveled to England. They saw that British servants were dignified and composed, and capable in their work. They considered them the best servants in the world. Therefore, they brought many people back to America. From then on, it was considered an honor to have British servants in American society. Colonel Lindbergh, the famous aviator, had a very capable British servant in his home. Even the chef and nanny were British. Therefore, his servants could be considered all British. American society not only liked to hire British servants, but also grooms, jockeys, golf club waiters, yacht captains, and bar managers were often hired from England. They received good treatment and particularly high wages. Unfortunately, they were also affected by the global economic panic. Many wealthy American families went bankrupt and no longer had the ability to hire British servants. Therefore, recently, a large number of British servants and chefs had to pack up and return home to try to find a livelihood in their own country.

Butterfly Dream in Lushan 144

— He Tianjian

Mount Lu is a scenic area in Jiangxi Province. It got its name because of the hermitage of Kuang Su and Lu Ao in the past. My friend Chen Xiaodie loves forests and springs and is not familiar with city life. He has explored the beauty of the Yellow Crane Tower and the wonders of the White Deer Cave. He went on a ten-day trip. The other day, he suddenly sent letters from the mountain to Ms. Xiaoman, Uncle Ya, and me. In his letter to Ms. Xiaoman, he mentioned a dream of seeing Zhimo and composed two poems to record it. Dream matters, although not believed by scientists, but spirits fly through Hessel, and Du Ling records them with poems. Grass grows in spring ponds, and Kang Le proclaims them in his poems. Considering the past, not everything is false. Moreover, wise literary men are born into heaven and become Buddhas. There is a reason for coming and going. With Zhimo's pure heart, how can we know that his spirits are not always in the human world and in heaven? Ms. Xiaoman said that Zhimo often traveled to the southwest, but he always regretted not having traveled enough in Mount Lu. Therefore, Xiaodie's dream has a reason. Xiaodie and Zhimo were close friends to the death, feeling life and remembering death, seeing things and thinking of people, how could he not turn it into a dream? I am recording his poem below. It is also a lyrical event in the literary world. Flying in the eight directions, Jizhou is narrow. I left Wuhui in the morning and arrived at Qiqiu in the evening. I was shaking my clothes on Peifeng Mountain. I was surprised to reach the end of the world. I spread my wings to catch the wild geese on the Yellow River. Who does not die on a carriage or boat? From now on, I can come and go by riding the air. I plan to circle the planet once. Magpie Hua's clouds and objects connect with Mount Lu. The wind horse and spirit car are easy to travel back and forth. Shaking hands, I clearly hear the children's words. In my dream, we are still brothers and friends. I love Mr. Xu the most in my life. Who pities Li Yi'an in this world? A volume of new words in Qingzhao's writing is still there. How difficult is it to die if the feelings are carved deep in the bone?

Stele Inscription of the Ningbo Renji Hospital 146

— Feng Duliang

Sea transport has opened, and human affairs have connected. Every day brings increasing complexity, and the spread of diseases and sores is also increasingly difficult to distinguish. Medical practitioners, unless they are thoroughly knowledgeable and insightful, will be unable to adapt and treat them. Western medicine has always emphasized experimentation. The slightest evidence must be thoroughly considered and investigated. The goal is to find the correct treatment and then prescribe medication. Even if there are breakthroughs, they are announced and proclaimed, making it a routine. This is because they can learn from each other and develop, and there is no intention of sticking to the old ways and closing off. Therefore, the art is easy to advance, and the effect is also slightly greater. Our people admire their achievements and gradually imitate them. Therefore, the hospital system arose. However, it is not easy to attract talent, and preparations cannot be simple. Extremely economical management requires huge amounts of money. If finances are insufficient, they often stop halfway. Those who seek profit by taking advantage of the situation can lightly deceive with thin receipts and poor operations. Poor planning leads to more harm. Those who claim to be broad and well-prepared, limited by the initial meticulous planning, often cannot help but exploit the sick and the poor. The sons of the wealthy cherish their health and will not mind bearing a small burden. However, the common people, whose clothes are not complete, once affected by the cold and heat, lack the funds to buy medicine. They either fill the ravines or languish in groans. Is this not the greatest pain of life? My Ningbo has tens of thousands of people, and the poor occupy the majority. Helping the wounded and relieving the distressed is not enough. Jin Jintingsun, a generous gentleman, roams the sea and is known for his prosperity. By nature, he enjoys relaxation and is deeply concerned about his old hometown. He is particularly diligent in giving gifts and tributes. When the autumn epidemic was rampant, the slaves and servants who were raised were often sick and died without seeing a doctor. Coffins were connected on the road. The gentleman looked at them and sighed, "Are these not the people of my neighborhood? How can I not do something for them?" He immediately gave up his family property to create what is called the temporary epidemic hospital. He widely sheltered the sick and the poor and exempted them from payment. Countless people were saved. When the epidemic subsided, the hospital was about to be abandoned. The gentleman punished himself for the past and wanted to expand the hospital and make it permanent. Fearing that he could not handle it alone, he consulted with Du Yuesheng. Du is a man from Shanghai, benevolent and outstanding, just like the gentleman. He agreed to assist the gentleman and conveyed the news to him. The gentleman's spirit grew stronger. He immediately bought land in the north of the city and began construction. The work began in July of the nineteenth year and ended in November of the twentieth year. Long corridors and deep rooms, wide houses and domed halls, were completed one after another. He then hired Dong Dingsong to preside over the hospital affairs, and everything was entrusted to him. Mr. Dong earnestly devoted himself to the work, without shirking labor. He used his hands to set up facilities, meticulously and thoroughly. Everything that a hospital should have was completed in a few months, without any obstacles. Before and after, he spent a total of 300,000 versions of money. All of this was due to the efforts of Mr. Du and Mr. Jin. The hospital was named Renji to show its righteous deeds. On the day of the completion, the wind was clear and the sun was bright. The public praised and admired the two gentlemen. Cai Mingcun and others admired their style and feared that it would be forgotten over time. They had Zhen Xu write the inscription. I believe that the meaning of life is to benefit the group, which is difficult. Mr. Du and Mr. Jin, who have wealth and position, do not enjoy themselves alone, but deeply pity the hardships of the people. They are as concerned as if they were guilty. They are anxious and thoughtful and must find a way to comfort and recommend them before they are relieved. This is the intention of benevolent gentlemen. Mr. Dong has been immersed in Western learning and has his own foundation. He is focused and determined, without changing from beginning to end. He will make this hospital bigger and bigger. I will not refuse to promote his virtues. I will record everything and write it on the hospital wall.

Record of a Couple Living Amidst War (Fifteen) 147

— Master of the Seeking Happiness Studio

Chapter Nine: The Special Train Ejects Guests with False Alarms; Sitting Cold in the Office, Turning to Stone in Reverie

But that big man who was always against him was still roaring. "You guys are wasting so much time talking nonsense to this kid. If it were up to me, I'd just kick him off the train. Who cares if he's real or fake?" As he spoke, he opened a big palm, as if he was about to grab An Yutian's collar. Fortunately, the others intervened and stopped the big man, saying, "Stop making trouble. Even if he's fake, give Guo face and let it go." Only then did the big man stop speaking. He lay down on the bed opposite An Yutian, fully clothed, and fell asleep. The remaining soldier had no bed and had to sit at An Yutian's feet, sharing a bed at opposite ends. An Yutian was in a dilemma and could only endure it for the time being. He leaned against the wall, feeling depressed for a while, and dozed off for a while. As the night deepened, he suddenly felt cold and couldn't help but feel more aggrieved. The old thoughts of hating the warlords were stirred up again. He deeply blamed Ye Zuozhang for his ineffective management, saying that even on the special train, it was so chaotic and disorderly, causing the guests to almost be insulted by those wolf-like guards. Where was the courtesy of respecting the virtuous? An Yutian was all misled by his wife, throwing a pearl into darkness. He spent half the night and early morning in annoyance, unable to sleep. He didn't even touch the drinking water, just endured the hunger and cold, losing his freedom, as if he was imprisoned in an army jail, suffering endless pain. Finally, the term of this sentence also had a time to end. The special train arrived at its destination at a little after 11 a.m. After Governor Ye got off the train, An Yutian was finally freed from the invisible surveillance by the guards and slipped off the train as if he was escaping. He suddenly remembered to find his wife. But at this time, there were not many people at the station. He couldn't guess if they had gotten off the train already. If they had left with Fifth Wife long ago, he would have nowhere to find them, wandering around like a homeless dog. He looked around the station, about to complain, when someone suddenly pushed him hard. He turned around and saw Mao Deshun dragging him anxiously and saying, "Secretary An, where on earth did you go? Last night, I heard the commander give those instructions to Deputy Guo, and I assumed you were with the commander in a carriage, so I told the wives and was relieved. But this morning, when the train was about to arrive, your wife told me to find you so we could get off the train together. It took me a lot of effort to find you, and I searched all the compartments and living rooms on the train. There was no sign of you. I wanted to ask Guo, but that kid stayed in Beijing for some other business and didn't come. I thought you had missed the train too. The wives were all very anxious and told me to search the station again. I only found you now. What's going on with you?"

Regarding the complete withdrawal of Japanese Marines, excluding the temporary garrison area, after the four-week deadline stipulated in the armistice agreement had passed, and then extended for another week, the Japanese side has yet to provide a definite indication of withdrawal. After receiving the report, we initially intended to notify the Joint Committee and convene a meeting if necessary. However, according to a report that the deployment was removed yesterday, the matter was terminated. Details of various reports are recorded below:

Full Withdrawal Indicated　Regarding the withdrawal of Japanese Marines from the area east of the Zhabei section of the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway and the eastern part of Sajing Port, Mr. Okazaki, the Japanese member of the Joint Committee, stated yesterday that the withdrawal date has not yet been decided. Due to the large number of Japanese residents in these two areas, withdrawal will likely occur only when the Japanese residents there are no longer experiencing panic. Da Mill, they will be withdrawn very soon. However, the locations of the Gong Da Mill, the Toyota Mill, and the Tongwen Academy are on roads built beyond the settlement boundaries (?).

Reply on the 13th　Regarding the reply from the Japanese member of the Joint Committee to the demand made by our member of the Joint Committee for the complete withdrawal of Japanese troops, it was rumored to be officially delivered today (the 11th).
